<h3><span class=\\'mw-headline\\' id=\\'Pronunciation\\'>Pronunciation</span><span class=\\'mw-editsection\\'><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>[</span><a href=\\'/w/index.php?title=just&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2\\' title=\\'Edit section", " ", "Pronunciation\\'>edit</a><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>]</span></span></h3>", <h3><span class=\\'mw-headline\\' id=\\'Pronunciation\\'>Pronunciation</span><span class=\\'mw-editsection\\'><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>[</span><a href=\\'/w/index.php?title=just&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2\\' title=\\'Edit section: Pronunciation\\'>edit</a><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>]</span></span></h3>"

<h3><span class=\\'mw-headline\\' id=\\'Etymology_1\\'>Etymology 1</span><span class=\\'mw-editsection\\'><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>[</span><a href=\\'/w/index.php?title=just&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3\\' title=\\'Edit section", " ", "Etymology 1\\'>edit</a><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>]</span></span></h3>", <h3><span class=\\'mw-headline\\' id=\\'Etymology_1\\'>Etymology 1</span><span class=\\'mw-editsection\\'><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>[</span><a href=\\'/w/index.php?title=just&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3\\' title=\\'Edit section: Etymology 1\\'>edit</a><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>]</span></span></h3>"
<p>From <span class=\\'etyl\\'><a href=\\'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English\\' class=\\'extiw\\' title=\\'w:Middle English\\'>Middle English</a></span> <i class=\\'Latn mention\\' lang=\\'enm\\'><a href=\\'/wiki/juste#Middle_English\\' title=\\'juste\\'>juste</a></i>, from <span class=\\'etyl\\'><a href=\\'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French\\' class=\\'extiw\\' title=\\'w:Old French\\'>Old French</a></span> <i class=\\'Latn mention\\' lang=\\'fro\\'><a href=\\'/wiki/juste#Old_French\\' title=\\'juste\\'>juste</a></i>, from <span class=\\'etyl\\'><a href=\\'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin\\' class=\\'extiw\\' title=\\'w:Latin\\'>Latin</a></span> <i class=\\'Latn mention\\' lang=\\'la\\'><a href=\\'/wiki/iustus#Latin\\' title=\\'iustus\\'>iūstus</a></i> <span class=\\'mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren\\'>(</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-double-quote\\'>“</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss\\'>just, lawful, rightful, true, due, proper, moderate</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-double-quote\\'>”</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren\\'>)</span>, from <span class=\\'etyl\\'><a href=\\'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Italic_language\\' class=\\'extiw\\' title=\\'w:Proto-Italic language\\'>Proto-Italic</a></span> <i class=\\'Latinx mention\\' lang=\\'itc-pro\\'><a href=\\'/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Italic/jowestos\\' title=\\'Reconstruction:Proto-Italic/jowestos\\'>*jowestos</a></i>, related to Latin <i class=\\'Latn mention\\' lang=\\'la\\'><a href=\\'/wiki/ius#Latin\\' title=\\'ius\\'>iūs</a></i> <span class=\\'mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren\\'>(</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-double-quote\\'>“</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss\\'>law, right</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-double-quote\\'>”</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren\\'>)</span>; ultimately from <span class=\\'etyl\\'><a href=\\'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language\\' class=\\'extiw\\' title=\\'w:Proto-Indo-European language\\'>Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class=\\'Latinx mention\\' lang=\\'ine-pro\\'><a href=\\'/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82yew-\\' title=\\'Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂yew-\\'>*h₂yew-</a></i>. <h4><span class=\\'mw-headline\\' id=\\'Interjection\\'>Interjection</span><span class=\\'mw-editsection\\'><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>[</span><a href=\\'/w/index.php?title=just&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15\\' title=\\'Edit section", " ", "Interjection\\'>edit</a><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>]</span></span></h4>", <h4><span class=\\'mw-headline\\' id=\\'Interjection\\'>Interjection</span><span class=\\'mw-editsection\\'><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>[</span><a href=\\'/w/index.php?title=just&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15\\' title=\\'Edit section: Interjection\\'>edit</a><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>]</span></span></h4>"

<p>Variation of <a href=\\'/wiki/joust\\' title=\\'joust\\'>joust</a>, presumably ultimately from <span class=\\'etyl\\'><a href=\\'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin\\' class=\\'extiw\\' title=\\'w:Latin\\'>Latin</a></span> <i class=\\'Latn mention\\' lang=\\'la\\'><a href=\\'/wiki/iuxta#Latin\\' title=\\'iuxta\\'>iuxta</a></i> <span class=\\'mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren\\'>(</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-double-quote\\'>“</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss\\'>near, besides</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-double-quote\\'>”</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren\\'>)</span>.", <p>Variation of <a href=\\'/wiki/joust\\' title=\\'joust\\'>joust</a>" , " presumably ultimately from <span class=\\'etyl\\'><a href=\\'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin\\' class=\\'extiw\\' title=\\'w:Latin\\'>Latin</a></span> <i class=\\'Latn mention\\' lang=\\'la\\'><a href=\\'/wiki/iuxta#Latin\\' title=\\'iuxta\\'>iuxta</a></i> <span class=\\'mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren\\'>(</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-double-quote\\'>“</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss\\'>near" , " besides</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-double-quote\\'>”</span><span class=\\'mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren\\'>)</span>."

<h3><span class=\\'mw-headline\\' id=\\'Verb_2\\'>Verb</span><span class=\\'mw-editsection\\'><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>[</span><a href=\\'/w/index.php?title=just&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51\\' title=\\'Edit section", " ", "Verb\\'>edit</a><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>]</span></span></h3>", <h3><span class=\\'mw-headline\\' id=\\'Verb_2\\'>Verb</span><span class=\\'mw-editsection\\'><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>[</span><a href=\\'/w/index.php?title=just&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51\\' title=\\'Edit section: Verb\\'>edit</a><span class=\\'mw-editsection-bracket\\'>]</span></span></h3>"
<p><strong class=\\'Latn headword\\' lang=\\'lv\\'>just</strong>&#160;(<a href=\\'/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive\\' title=\\'Appendix:Glossary\\'><i>tr</i></a>.,&#160;<i>1st <a lang=\\'lv\\'>just</strong>&#160;(<a href=\\'/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive\\' title=\\'Appendix:Glossary\\'><i>tr</i></a>." , "&#160;<i>1st <a href=\\'/wiki/conjugation\\' title=\\'conjugation\\'>conj</a></i>." , " <i><a href=\\'/wiki/present_tense\\' title=\\'present tense\\'>pres</a></i>. <b><span class=\\'Latn\\' lang=\\'lv\\'><a </p>", </p>"
<ol><li>to <a href=\\'/wiki/feel\\' title=\\'feel\\'>feel</a> <span class=\\'gloss-brac\\'>(</span><span class=\\'gloss-content\\'>to <a href=\\'/wiki/perceive\\' title=\\'perceive\\'>perceive</a> with one\\'s <a href=\\'/wiki/sense\\' title=\\'sense\\'>sense</a> <a href=\\'/wiki/organ\\' title=\\'organ\\'>organs</a></span><span class=\\'gloss-brac\\'>)</span>", <ol><li>to <a href=\\'/wiki/feel\\' title=\\'feel\\'>feel</a> <span class=\\'gloss-brac\\'>(</span><span class=\\'gloss-content\\'>to <a href=\\'/wiki/perceive\\' title=\\'perceive\\'>perceive</a> with one\\'s <a href=\\'/wiki/sense\\' title=\\'sense\\'>sense</a> <a href=\\'/wiki/organ\\' title=\\'organ\\'>organs</a></span><span class=\\'gloss-brac\\'>)</span>"
<dl><dd><div class=\\'h-usage-example\\'><i class=\\'Latn mention e-example\\' lang=\\'lv\\'><b>just</b> aukstumu, karstumu, sāpes</i> ― <span class=\\'e-translation\\'>to <b>feel</b> cold, heat, pain</span></div></dd>", <dl><dd><div class=\\'h-usage-example\\'><i class=\\'Latn mention e-example\\' lang=\\'lv\\'><b>just</b> aukstumu" , " karstumu" , " sāpes</i> ― <span class=\\'e-translation\\'>to <b>feel</b> cold" , " heat" , " pain</span></div></dd>"
<dd><div class=\\'h-usage-example\\'><i class=\\'Latn mention e-example\\' lang=\\'lv\\'>tā, ka <b>nejūt</b> zemi zem kājām</i> ― <span class=\\'e-translation\\'>such that s/he doesn\\'t <b>feel</b> the earth under his/her feet (= very fast)</span></div></dd></dl></li>", <dd><div class=\\'h-usage-example\\'><i class=\\'Latn mention e-example\\' lang=\\'lv\\'>tā" , " ka <b>nejūt</b> zemi zem kājām</i> ― <span class=\\'e-translation\\'>such that s/he doesn\\'t <b>feel</b> the earth under his/her feet (= very fast)</span></div></dd></dl></li>"
